About the Business
	•	Business name: Aqua Force
	•	Services offered:
	•	Residential and commercial window cleaning
	•	Interior and exterior window cleaning
	•	Gutter cleaning
	•	Fascia &amp; soffit cleaning
	•	I want the tone to feel:
	•	Professional, premium, and trustworthy
	•	Clean, simple, and modern
	•	Customer-focused

Branding
	•	Use a gold, white, and black color scheme.
	•	Theme should feel luxurious, high-quality, and sharp.
	•	Include a strong hero section with a call to action like:
	•	“Crystal-clear results every time.”
	•	“Book your clean with Aqua Force today.”

Pages to Include
	1.	Home
	•	Overview of services
	•	Why choose Aqua Force
	•	Testimonials section
	•	Call-to-action buttons
	2.	Services
	•	Detailed descriptions of:
	•	Window cleaning
	•	Interior &amp; exterior cleaning
	•	Gutter cleaning
	•	Fascia &amp; soffit cleaning
	•	Any add-on options

	•	Story of Aqua Force
	•	What makes us different (local, reliable, insured, premium service)
	4.	Gallery
	•	Before/after images
	5.	Contact
	•	Phone number, email, service areas
	•	Contact form
	•	Option to request a quote

Extra Features
	•	Add a sticky header with navigation.
	•	Add SEO-optimized text for window cleaning and gutter cleaning in my local area.
	•	Make the site mobile-friendly, clean, and elegant.
	•	Include booking buttons throughout the site.

	•	Headings
